SUPPLEMENTAL ANALYSIS: MISUSE OF PROFESSIONAL AUTHORITY
As a caseworker for the Kent County Prosecutor’s Office, Emily Watson holds a position of authority,
requiring adherence to the highest ethical standards, particularly in matters involving family law.
However, Emily has exploited her professional knowledge and access to legal systems to manipulate
the custody process, alienate LDW from me, and obstruct fair and cooperative co-parenting. Below is
a detailed analysis of how Emily’s misuse of her professional authority directly undermines LDW’s
best interests and my parental rights, necessitating immediate court intervention.
1. Exploitation of Legal Knowledge to Weaponize PPOs and Legal Claims
Emily has repeatedly used her understanding of legal procedures and her access to legal systems to
file baseless Personal Protection Orders (PPOs) and unfounded legal claims against me. Notable
examples include:
Filing Unfounded PPO Complaints: Emily has filed multiple PPO complaints without valid grounds,
knowing the burden such complaints place on me as a co-parent. These filings were often based on
fabricated allegations, such as claims of harassment stemming from my lawful attempts to communicate
about LDW. For example:

--- PAGE 68 ---

October 2024: Emily alleged that I violated the PPO by contacting her regarding LDW’s health and
well-being, even though my communications were appropriate and focused on parenting matters.
These actions align with patterns of parental alienation, as defined in Rappleye v. Rappleye, 183
Mich. App. 396 (1990), where the court emphasized that false legal claims designed to restrict
parental access harm the child’s best interests.
Leveraging PPOs to Avoid Co-Parenting: Emily has explicitly used PPOs as a means to avoid necessary
co-parenting communication, violating LDW’s right to a balanced relationship with both parents. This
behavior contradicts MCL 722.23(j), which prioritizes fostering a close parent-child relationship
with both parents.
2. Access to and Misuse of Confidential Information
Emily’s professional position grants her access to sensitive and confidential information that she
has improperly leveraged to gain an advantage in custody proceedings. Examples include:
Accessing and Using Private Health Records: Emily allegedly accessed my personal health records,
including mental health treatment history, without authorization. She used this information to
falsely portray me as unfit to parent, despite my demonstrated stability and commitment to LDW’s
well-being. This constitutes a violation of my privacy and professional ethics.
Fabricating Allegations Based on Misused Data: Emily has used her insider knowledge to fabricate and
bolster allegations against me, such as claims of drug abuse or instability, which lack evidence and
rely solely on manipulated interpretations of data she accessed.
These actions reflect a breach of professional ethics as outlined in Michigan Rules of Professional
Conduct (MRPC 8.4), which prohibit conduct involving dishonesty, fraud, or misrepresentation,
particularly when it directly harms the well-being of a minor.
3. Manipulation of Custody Proceedings
Emily’s legal knowledge has enabled her to manipulate custody proceedings by presenting misleading
evidence and exploiting procedural advantages. Specific concerns include:
Staging Evidence to Undermine My Parenting: Emily has reportedly staged incidents to create false
narratives about my parenting fitness, such as:
October 15, 2023: Emily alleged that she discovered a straw with suspected cocaine residue in her
home, insinuating that I was responsible. This baseless accusation has been repeatedly referenced
despite a complete lack of evidence, damaging my reputation and influencing custody decisions.
Delaying or Withholding Court-Mandated Information: Emily has repeatedly delayed or refused to
provide essential documents, such as medical records and insurance information for LDW. For example:
May 28, 2024: Emily provided only partial medical records despite a court order requiring full
disclosure. Her failure to cooperate hindered my ability to make informed decisions about LDW’s
health, violating MCL 722.23(c), which requires both parents to demonstrate the capacity to provide
for the child’s medical needs.
4. Abuse of Position to Mislead the Court
Emily’s professional role has given her undue credibility in the eyes of the Court, which she has
exploited to misrepresent facts and mislead the Court about her own actions and fitness as a parent.
Examples include:
Portraying False Stability: Emily has misrepresented her household environment as safe and stable,
despite the presence of her brother Cody Watson, who has a history of violent behavior and substance
abuse. Her professional authority has allowed her to downplay these risks, directly endangering LDW.
Leveraging Her Position to Evade Scrutiny: Emily has used her role to deflect accountability for her
alienating behavior, such as:
Withholding LDW during my parenting time on multiple occasions.
Falsely portraying my efforts to communicate as harassment or interference.
This misuse of professional standing contradicts Ireland v. Smith, 451 Mich. 457 (1996), which
emphasizes the importance of transparency and honesty in custody disputes to protect the child’s
best interests.
5. Ethical Concerns Regarding Parental Alienation
As a caseworker, Emily has professional knowledge of the damaging effects of parental alienation on
a child’s emotional well-being. Despite this, she has engaged in behaviors that foster alienation,
including:

--- PAGE 69 ---

Blocking Communication: Emily has routinely refused to facilitate video chats or phone calls between
me and LDW, undermining our bond. Her knowledge of the psychological impact of such actions makes
this behavior particularly egregious.
Encouraging False Narratives: Emily’s family, under her influence, has made disparaging remarks
about me in LDW’s presence, contributing to an environment of alienation. This behavior aligns with
the court’s findings in Shade v. Wright, 291 Mich. App. 17 (2010), where fostering a child’s
alienation from a parent was considered detrimental to the child’s best interests.
6. Legal Precedents Supporting Custody Modification
The following legal precedents highlight the Court’s responsibility to address Emily’s misuse of
professional authority and its impact on LDW:
Vodvarka v. Grasmeyer, 259 Mich. App. 499 (2003): Establishes that a substantial change in
circumstances, such as parental alienation or misuse of authority, justifies custody modification.
Rappleye v. Rappleye, 183 Mich. App. 396 (1990): Emphasizes the harm caused by alienation and false
legal claims in custody disputes.
Phillips v. Jordan, 241 Mich. App. 17 (2000): Recognizes the court’s obligation to protect children
from inappropriate discipline and unsafe household environments.
Shade v. Wright, 291 Mich. App. 17 (2010): Highlights the impact of alienating behavior on a child’s
emotional health and the need for court intervention.

respectfully request the Court to:
Reevaluate Custody Arrangements: Modify custody to grant primary physical custody to me, ensuring
LDW’s safety and emotional well-being.
Mandate Supervised Parenting Time: Require Emily’s parenting time to be supervised until her misuse
of authority and alienating behaviors are addressed.
Appoint a Guardian ad Litem: Assign a GAL to assess Emily’s actions and their impact on LDW’s well-
being.
Issue Protective Orders: Restrict Emily’s access to my personal records and ensure that confidential
information is not misused in custody proceedings.
CONCLUSION
Emily’s misuse of professional authority not only undermines the integrity of the custody process
but also places LDW’s well-being at significant risk. Her actions demonstrate a pattern of
alienation, manipulation, and disregard for ethical standards, which directly harm LDW’s emotional
and psychological stability. A custody modification is necessary to protect LDW and ensure his right
to a healthy, balanced relationship with both parents.

GROUNDS FOR CUSTODY MODIFICATION UNDER MCL 722.27
1. Proper Cause or Change in Circumstances (MCL 722.27)
Michigan law requires a substantial change in circumstances or proper cause to modify custody. As
held in Vodvarka v. Grasmeyer, 259 Mich. App. 499 (2003), these changes must significantly impact
the child’s well-being. The Defendant’s consistent alienation, refusal to comply with parenting time
orders, and misuse of legal processes create instability and emotional harm to LDW. These actions
justify custody modification to protect LDW’s long-term well-being.
ANALYSIS OF BEST INTEREST FACTORS UNDER MCL 722.23
Factor (a): Love, Affection, and Emotional Ties (MCL 722.23(a))
I have built a strong emotional bond with LDW through shared routines, enriching activities, and a
supportive home environment. Conversely, Emily has obstructed my ability to maintain this bond by
withholding parenting time and blocking communication. Shade v. Wright, 291 Mich. App. 17 (2010)
recognizes that alienation efforts undermine the child’s emotional ties with both parents,
warranting intervention.
Factor (b): Capacity to Provide Guidance and Love (MCL 722.23(b))
I actively engage in LDW’s development by providing emotional support, teaching values, and
fostering creativity. Emily’s refusal to share health updates and engage in cooperative parenting
violates the standard set in Ireland v. Smith, 451 Mich. 457 (1996), which emphasizes the importance

--- PAGE 72 ---

of co-parenting for the child’s emotional health.
Factor (c): Capacity to Meet Material Needs (MCL 722.23(c))
I am financially stable, providing LDW with a well-maintained home, clothing, and nutritious meals.
Defendant’s failure to properly prepare LDW for exchanges and dismissiveness toward his medical
needs contradicts the principles outlined in Baker v. Baker, 411 Mich. 567 (1981), where meeting the
child’s physical needs is paramount.
Factor (d): Stability of the Environment (MCL 722.23(d))
My home offers LDW a stable, nurturing environment. In contrast, Emily’s frequent absences and
reliance on third parties introduce instability. Brown v. Loveman, 260 Mich. App. 576 (2004)
confirms that disruptions to a child’s continuity are grounds for modifying custody.
Factor (j): Willingness to Foster the Parent-Child Relationship (MCL 722.23(j))
I have consistently encouraged LDW’s relationship with Emily, while she has repeatedly alienated LDW
from me, including withholding parenting time and failing to communicate. Pickering v. Pickering,
268 Mich. App. 1 (2005) establishes that such actions justify modifying custody to prioritize the
child’s relationship with both parents.
ADDITIONAL LEGAL SUPPORT FOR FINANCIAL CLAIMS
MCL 552.17 – Modification of Child Support
The Defendant has failed to disclose supplemental income sources, including rent from family members
and support from her child’s father, Austin Muratori. As held in Hogg v. Hogg, 50 Mich. App. 508
(1973), courts may impute income or recalculate support when a parent misrepresents financial
circumstances.
MCR 3.208(C) – Income Disclosure Requirements
Under this rule, parties are required to provide complete and accurate financial information.
Emily’s failure to report these income sources skews the child support calculation, resulting in an
unjust financial burden on me. Burba v. Burba, 461 Mich. 637 (2000) emphasizes that support must
reflect both parents’ actual financial contributions.
RELIEF REQUESTED
Modify Custody:
Restore 50/50 custody to ensure LDW has balanced, meaningful contact with both parents, protecting
his emotional and developmental needs as outlined in MCL 722.23.
Enforce Parenting Time:
Penalize the Defendant for repeated violations under MCL 722.27a(11), ensuring compliance with
court-ordered parenting schedules.
Recalculate Child Support:
Reevaluate support based on accurate income disclosure under MCL 552.17 and MCR 3.208(C), correcting
prior miscalculations caused by the Defendant’s omissions.
Address Parental Alienation:
Mandate counseling for both parties to mitigate the harmful effects of alienation, per Eldred v.
Eldred, 246 Mich. App. 142 (2001).
Guardian ad Litem Appointment:
Appoint a GAL under MCL 722.24 to assess LDW’s well-being and address the ongoing harm caused by
alienation.
Immediate Temporary Relief:
Grant temporary custody modifications to stabilize LDW’s emotional health during these proceedings,
consistent with the principles in Vodvarka v. Grasmeyer.
CONCLUSION
The Defendant’s repeated actions to alienate LDW, obstruct parenting time, and misrepresent
financial information significantly impact his emotional and developmental well-being. The proposed
modifications are necessary to safeguard LDW’s best interests and restore stability in his life.

Emotional Impact of Parental Alienation on LDW

disrupts a child’s sense of security, emotional development, and long-term mental health. The

emotional toll of Emily’s actions on LDW has been profound, and the ongoing alienation continues to

the parental roles Emily is attempting to manipulate.
Symptoms of Anxiety: LDW has displayed symptoms consistent with heightened anxiety, including crying

Michael Bone, a leading expert in parental alienation, notes that such behaviors are hallmark signs
of the stress caused by alienation.

leaving him distressed and unsettled during transitions.
2. Healthcare Neglect
Failure to Address Medical Concerns:
Emily has repeatedly neglected LDW’s medical needs, ignoring signs of illness or injury and refusing
to take appropriate action.
Example: On June 15, 2024, LDW returned from Emily’s care with severe rashes on his face and body.
Despite my repeated inquiries, Emily dismissed the condition as "minor" and refused to seek medical
advice.
Example: On October 4, 2024, LDW arrived with a large, unexplained bruise on his leg. When asked for
an explanation, Emily gave vague responses, refusing to acknowledge the need for follow-up care.
Missed Dental Appointments:
LDW has been overdue for his first dental appointment since February 2024, despite recommendations
from his physician. Emily has taken no action to schedule or prioritize this critical aspect of
LDW’s health.
Unilateral Medical Decisions Without Consultation:
On May 15, 2024, Emily vaccinated LDW without informing or consulting me, despite the joint custody
arrangement. This not only undermines co-parenting but also demonstrates her disregard for
collaborative decision-making regarding LDW’s health.
3. Emotional and Developmental Neglect
Inadequate Attention to Emotional Needs:
Emily has failed to address LDW’s emotional well-being during transitions and parenting exchanges,
causing him unnecessary distress.
Example: On October 20, 2024, during a parenting exchange, Emily allowed her father, Albert Watson,
to forcibly remove LDW from my arms in a hostile manner. This aggressive behavior in LDW’s presence
created a traumatic experience for him.
Denial of Communication:
Emily frequently denies my attempts to maintain contact with LDW during her parenting weeks,
depriving him of emotional support and continuity with both parents.
Example: On June 1, 2024, and September 12, 2024, Emily refused to allow scheduled video calls,
claiming LDW “doesn’t want to talk.” These actions disrupt LDW’s sense of connection and emotional
stability.
Interruption of Routines:
Emily has shown little regard for maintaining consistent routines for LDW, which are critical for
his development at a young age.
Example: Emily’s decision to remove LDW from his daycare at Kids Fun Learning Center in March 2024
disrupted his established routine and social interactions, negatively impacting his emotional and
cognitive development.
4. Neglect of Safety
Exposure to Unsafe Individuals:
Emily has allowed her brother, Cody Watson, who has a documented history of violence and substance
abuse, to remain involved in LDW’s life, despite my concerns for his safety.
Example: On May 28, 2024, I raised concerns about Cody Watson’s behavior, including reports of
substance use and aggression, yet Emily continued to allow him access to LDW without addressing
these risks.
Hostile Exchanges:
Emily’s father, Albert Watson, has been involved in multiple aggressive incidents during parenting

--- PAGE 91 ---

exchanges, creating an unsafe and emotionally volatile environment for LDW.
Example: On October 20, 2024, Albert Watson forcibly removed LDW from my arms during an exchange,
shouting and throwing a PPO violation into my vehicle. This hostile behavior exposed LDW to
unnecessary emotional trauma.
Failure to Supervise:
LDW has returned from Emily’s care with unexplained injuries on several occasions, raising questions
about the adequacy of her supervision.
Example: On October 4, 2024, LDW had a visible bruise and a cut on his leg, yet Emily offered no
credible explanation for how the injuries occurred.
5. Neglect of Co-Parenting Responsibilities
Withholding Parenting Time:
Emily has repeatedly withheld LDW from me without justification, violating court orders and
depriving LDW of critical bonding time with his father.
Example: Between March 26 and May 2, 2024, Emily withheld LDW for 37 consecutive days, disrupting
our bond and creating emotional distress for LDW.
Failure to Share Information:
Emily consistently withholds updates about LDW’s health, education, and daily life, undermining my
ability to participate fully in his upbringing.
Example: On November 19, 2024, I was not informed about LDW’s doctor’s appointment or his
vaccinations, leaving me unable to provide input or support.
Refusal to Collaborate on Major Decisions:
Emily has dismissed or ignored my efforts to collaborate on decisions that affect LDW’s well-being,
such as daycare arrangements and holiday plans.
Example: On May 9, 2024, Emily rejected my proposal for consistent daycare across parenting weeks,
prioritizing her preferences over LDW’s stability.
Conclusion
Emily’s ongoing neglect of LDW’s basic needs, safety, and emotional well-being underscores her
inability to prioritize his best interests. These examples highlight a troubling pattern of behavior
that places LDW at risk and necessitates immediate intervention. My proactive efforts to address
LDW’s needs, coupled with my consistent advocacy for his safety and stability, further emphasize the
necessity of a custody modification to ensure his long-term well-being.
AFFIDAVIT IN SUPPORT OF MOTION TO MODIFY CUSTODY, PARENTING TIME, AND CHILD SUPPORT
Plaintiff: Andrew J. Pigors
Defendant: Emily A. Watson
I, Andrew J. Pigors, affirm that the information contained in this affidavit is true to the best of
my knowledge and belief.
I. INTRODUCTION
This affidavit is submitted in support of my motion to modify custody, increase parenting time, and
recalculate child support for my minor son, LDW (born November 9, 2022). Since May 2024, the Friend
of the Court (FOC) recommended a 50/50 custody arrangement, which reflected the balanced parenting
environment I have continuously provided. However, since that recommendation, the Defendant, Emily
Watson, has escalated alienating behavior, failed to meet LDW’s basic needs, and demonstrated moral
lapses that jeopardize LDW’s well-being and emotional development.
In contrast, I have remained steadfast in providing LDW with stability, emotional support, and a
nurturing environment tailored to his growth. This affidavit details specific incidents of concern,
aligned with the 12 Best Interest Factors under MCL 722.23, to demonstrate why a modification of the
current custody arrangement is urgently required.
II. PATTERN OF BEHAVIOR: EMILY WATSON
1. Parental Alienation
Encouraging Rejection of Me as LDW’s Father:
Emily has undermined my role as LDW’s father by instructing him to refer to her new partner as
"Daddy" while discouraging him from using the same term for me. This deliberate act confuses LDW and
creates emotional barriers between us.
Defamation and False Allegations:

--- PAGE 92 ---

Emily has falsely accused me of substance abuse, poisoning her, and neglecting LDW without evidence.
These allegations were intended to damage my reputation, alienate me from LDW, and manipulate court
proceedings.
Blocking Communication:
Emily routinely denies scheduled video calls with LDW, including incidents on June 1, 2024, and
September 12, 2024, claiming he "doesn’t want to talk" without providing evidence. Additionally, she
has failed to share updates on LDW’s health and milestones, including withholding information about
vaccinations on November 19, 2024.
Withholding Parenting Time:
Emily has withheld LDW during court-ordered parenting time, including:
March 26 – May 2, 2024 (37 consecutive days)
October 20 – November 12, 2024 (23 consecutive days)
2. Neglect of LDW’s Basic Needs
Healthcare Neglect:
Emily has failed to schedule LDW’s first dental appointment, despite it being overdue since February
2024, and has dismissed medical concerns such as rashes and unexplained bruises.
Unexplained Injuries:
LDW has frequently arrived at exchanges with visible injuries, including:
October 4, 2024: LDW had a large bruise on his leg. Emily dismissed concerns without explanation.
June 15, 2024: LDW had severe rashes that Emily failed to address.
Inadequate Preparation:
LDW often arrives at parenting exchanges without weather-appropriate clothing, shoes, or basic
necessities. On only one occasion (October 17, 2024) did Emily provide proper clothing after I
raised concerns in AppClose communications.
3. Manipulative Legal and Financial Tactics
Misrepresentation of Financial Information:
Emily has exaggerated insurance costs while failing to disclose rental income from her brother, Cody
Watson, who resides in her home.
Misuse of PPOs:
Emily has weaponized PPOs to restrict my access to LDW, including an incident on October 20, 2024,
where his father, Albert Watson, served a PPO violation during a parenting exchange in an aggressive
and mocking manner.
False Allegations:
Emily accused me of substance abuse during exchanges, poisoning her with arsenic, and harassment,
all of which were dismissed for lack of evidence.
4. Hostile and Aggressive Behavior
Albert Watson’s Aggression:
Albert Watson has engaged in hostile behavior during exchanges, including:
November 2023: Physically assaulting me at 2160 Garland.
October 20, 2024: Forcibly removing LDW from my arms during an exchange.
Cody Watson’s Intimidation:
Cody Watson has exhibited threatening behavior, including road harassment on September 20, 2024,
violating the PPO and endangering LDW.
III. APPLICATION OF THE 12 BEST INTEREST FACTORS
The following is an analysis of the 12 Best Interest Factors under MCL 722.23, demonstrating why a
custody modification is in LDW’s best interests.
(a) Love, Affection, and Emotional Ties
I have fostered a deep, nurturing bond with LDW through daily routines, creative activities, and
consistent emotional support. Emily’s alienation tactics actively disrupt this bond, causing LDW
confusion and emotional distress.
(b) Capacity to Provide Guidance and Love
I prioritize LDW’s development through educational activities, instilling values of empathy and
independence. Emily’s refusal to collaborate on parenting decisions undermines these efforts.
(c) Capacity to Provide Material Needs

--- PAGE 93 ---

I maintain stable employment, have renovated my home for LDW’s comfort, and provide for all his
material needs. Emily has demonstrated negligence by failing to schedule dental visits, dismissing
medical concerns, and sending LDW to exchanges unprepared.
(d) Stability and Continuity
My home offers LDW a permanent, stable environment. Emily’s repeated withholding of LDW, coupled
with hostile exchanges involving his father and brother, disrupts his sense of stability.
(e) Permanence of the Custodial Home
My home is a safe, nurturing environment specifically tailored to LDW’s needs. Emily’s home is
compromised by the presence of Cody Watson, whose history of violence and substance abuse poses a
safety risk.
(f) Moral Fitness
I consistently model integrity, respect, and responsibility for LDW. Emily’s false accusations,
alienation tactics, and allowance of unsafe influences like Cody Watson demonstrate a lack of moral
fitness.
(g) Mental and Physical Health
I am in excellent mental and physical health, enabling me to provide a stable and supportive
environment. Emily’s erratic behavior, including her involvement in confrontational exchanges,
raises concerns about her ability to prioritize LDW’s well-being.
(h) Home, School, and Community Record
I actively engage LDW in positive social and community activities. Emily’s refusal to collaborate on
extracurricular activities hinders his social development.
(i) Reasonable Preference of the Child
While LDW is too young to express a preference, his behavior during exchanges—showing joy and
comfort in my care—indicates a strong attachment to me.
(j) Willingness to Facilitate the Parent-Child Relationship
I have consistently encouraged LDW’s relationship with Emily. In contrast, her alienation tactics
obstruct my relationship with LDW, violating this factor.
(k) Domestic Violence
Albert Watson’s aggression during exchanges and Cody Watson’s intimidation raise significant safety
concerns for LDW in Emily’s home.
(l) Any Other Relevant Factor
Emily’s abuse of her professional knowledge as a caseworker to manipulate legal proceedings
demonstrates unethical behavior that undermines LDW’s best interests.
IV. REQUEST FOR RELIEF
Based on the above, I respectfully request the Court:
Modify Custody to restore a 50/50 arrangement or grant me primary custody.
Increase Parenting Time to reestablish my bond with LDW.
Recalculate Child Support to reflect Emily’s true financial situation.
Mandate Co-Parenting Counseling to address communication barriers and alienation.
Order a Guardian ad Litem to evaluate LDW’s best interests and safety concerns in Emily’s household.

Emotional Impact of Parental Alienation on LDW
Parental alienation is one of the most damaging behaviors a parent can exhibit, as it deeply
disrupts a child’s sense of security, emotional development, and long-term mental health. The
emotional toll of Emily’s actions on LDW has been profound, and the ongoing alienation continues to
endanger his emotional well-being and developmental trajectory. Below, I outline the specific ways
in which parental alienation is affecting LDW emotionally, with examples from documented incidents.
1. Heightened Anxiety and Emotional Insecurity
Confusion in Relationships: Emily’s deliberate attempts to alienate LDW from me, such as encouraging
him to call her new partner "Daddy" while discouraging him from using that term for me, create deep
emotional confusion. LDW, at his young age, is forming critical attachments, and these conflicting

in the future.
5. Long-Term Psychological Harm
Erosion of Parental Bond: Parental alienation creates a rift between a child and the alienated
parent that can have lasting consequences. By actively undermining my relationship with LDW, Emily

Research Insight: Studies on parental alienation show that children subjected to such behaviors are
at higher risk for depression, anxiety, low self-esteem, and difficulty forming trusting
relationships later in life. LDW is at risk of internalizing the conflict and alienation, which
could impact his emotional health for years to come.

self-worth. By alienating LDW from me, Emily is denying him the opportunity to form a balanced sense
of self, which could lead to identity confusion and emotional struggles as he grows older.

Despite Emily’s efforts to alienate LDW, I dedicate myself to rebuilding our bond through meaningful

his sense of security and love.

Lack of Updates: Emily frequently withholds critical updates about LDW’s health, education, and
daily routine, preventing Andrew from being an informed and active co-parent.
Example: On November 19, 2024, Emily failed to inform Andrew about LDW’s vaccinations in advance,
excluding him from important medical decisions.
Vague Explanations: Emily has provided incomplete or evasive responses to questions about LDW’s
injuries, illnesses, and milestones, leaving Andrew with insufficient information to ensure LDW’s
well-being.
10. Emotional Manipulation
Encouraging LDW to Call Another Man "Daddy": Emily has instructed LDW to call her new partner
"Daddy," which creates confusion and emotional harm by undermining Andrew’s parental role.
Discouraging Positive Attachment: Emily has made disparaging comments about Andrew in LDW’s
presence, further alienating him and disrupting his emotional development.
Conclusion
Emily Watson’s neglectful behaviors—including her failure to address LDW’s healthcare needs, provide
proper clothing, ensure safe environments, and prioritize emotional well-being—demonstrate a
consistent disregard for LDW’s best interests. Her actions expose LDW to unnecessary risks, disrupt
his sense of security, and hinder his developmental and emotional growth. Immediate intervention is
necessary to address these issues and protect LDW from further harm.

developmental well-being. My contributions as a father demonstrate a consistent commitment to
providing a loving, stable, and supportive environment where LDW can thrive.
1. Emotional Bond and Attachment
Active and Loving Presence: I have fostered a deep and nurturing bond with LDW by being actively
involved in his life. I ensure he feels loved, valued, and secure in my presence.

Example: LDW and I share bedtime routines, including reading books and singing songs, which give him

at exchanges, reflect his strong emotional attachment to me.

safety I provide.
2. Providing a Stable and Nurturing Home Environment

friendly, safe, and welcoming. This includes:
Creating a special room for LDW with a bed, shelves of books, educational toys, a piano, and a drum
set to encourage creativity and learning.
Renovating my home from the pipes to the roof to ensure a safe and clean living space.
Consistency in Routines: I maintain consistent daily routines to foster LDW’s sense of stability.
Example: We regularly shop for groceries together, prepare meals, and enjoy shared activities like
art projects and trips to the park.
3. Commitment to LDW’s Health and Well-Being
Proactive Healthcare Decisions: I ensure LDW receives prompt and appropriate medical care whenever
necessary.
Example: I prioritize "better safe than sorry" medical decisions, such as addressing rashes,
unexplained bruises, and other health concerns immediately.
Example: I proposed testing for a potential peanut allergy when LDW displayed a rash, emphasizing my

grooming to ensure his overall well-being.

care.

development.
Example: I provide him with art supplies like crayons, markers, and paints to encourage creativity
and learning.
Example: I teach LDW empathy, independence, and respect for the environment, such as showing him not
to litter and to care for others.

build social connections in a safe and supportive environment.
Example: We regularly visit local parks, the library, and community events to expose him to
enriching experiences.
5. Financial Responsibility and Stability
Steady Employment: I maintain full-time employment at Shape Corporation, where I have recently
earned a promotion. This demonstrates my financial stability and ability to provide for LDW.
Fulfilling Financial Obligations: I have consistently paid child support and arrears, as well as
other financial contributions for LDW’s benefit.
Example: Despite financial challenges, I have ensured LDW has clothing, shoes, and toys to meet all
his needs.
Example: I prioritize spending on LDW, including purchasing shoes, socks, coats, and other
essentials when Emily fails to provide them.

Prioritizing LDW’s Needs Over My Own: I have made personal sacrifices to ensure LDW’s well-being,
including dedicating my free time to improve his living environment and advocating for his best
interests in court.

Example: I have declined personal outings and vacations to focus on spending quality time with LDW
and improving his home.
Efforts to Co-Parent: I have consistently reached out to Emily to collaborate on LDW’s health,

stability and predictability.
Example: I encouraged video calls and updates to maintain continuity during off-weeks, which Emily

7. Emotional and Psychological Support

Example: I emphasize positive reinforcement, helping LDW develop confidence and resilience.

advocate for LDW’s right to a balanced and loving relationship with both parents.

nurturing home environment to advocating for his health and safety, I consistently prioritize LDW’s
emotional, physical, and developmental needs. These contributions reflect my dedication to fostering
a stable, loving, and enriching environment where LDW can thrive.

Emily Watson’s Alienating Acts
Encouraging LDW to Reject Me:
Instructed LDW to call her new partner “Daddy” while discouraging him from referring to me as

Undermined my role as a parent through false narratives and manipulative language.
Blocking Communication:
Denied scheduled video calls, citing LDW “doesn’t want to talk,” with no supporting evidence (e.g.,
June 1, 2024, and September 12, 2024).
Failed to share critical updates about LDW’s health, education, and activities, such as doctor’s
visits and vaccinations (e.g., November 19, 2024).
Withholding Parenting Time:
Withheld LDW from March 26 to May 2, 2024, for 37 consecutive days without legal justification.
Withheld LDW again from October 20 to November 12, 2024, denying me meaningful time during Halloween
and his birthday.
Fostering Hostile Environments:
Involved his father, Albert Watson, in aggressive and confrontational exchanges, including forcibly
taking LDW from my arms (e.g., October 20, 2024).
Allowed Cody Watson, with a history of substance abuse and aggression, to be present in LDW’s
environment.
Neglecting Co-Parenting Responsibilities:
Refused to attend co-parenting classes or engage in meaningful dialogue to collaborate on LDW’s
needs (e.g., September 10, 2024).
Ignored or dismissed my concerns about LDW’s health, safety, and developmental needs, such as a
potential peanut allergy and emotional regression.
Defamation and False Allegations:
Accused me of substance abuse, poisoning her with arsenic, and criminal behavior, all without
evidence.
Filed frivolous police reports and PPO violations, creating unnecessary tension and portraying me
negatively.
Limiting Emotional Bonding:
Denied opportunities for shared holiday experiences, such as Halloween and LDW’s birthday.
Refused to allow consistent contact, such as weekly video calls, during off-weeks.

Failing to Protect LDW from Conflict:
Exposed LDW to emotionally volatile situations, such as aggressive confrontations with his father
during parenting exchanges.

Encouraging LDW’s Relationship with Emily:
Consistently emphasized the importance of LDW’s bond with both parents.
Refrained from speaking negatively about Emily in LDW’s presence, prioritizing his emotional
stability.
Facilitating Communication:
Regularly reached out to Emily to collaborate on parenting matters, such as daycare consistency,
healthcare, and holiday plans.
Proposed weekly video calls during off-weeks to maintain emotional continuity for LDW (e.g., June 1,
2024).
Maximizing Parenting Time:
Made every effort to spend quality time with LDW, engaging him in educational and bonding activities
such as art projects, park visits, and bedtime routines.
Actively sought court intervention to regain lost parenting time and protect LDW’s right to a
balanced relationship with both parents.
Creating a Safe and Stable Environment:
Renovated my home to ensure it is child-friendly, safe, and nurturing, complete with a special room
for LDW filled with books, toys, and musical instruments.
Provided LDW with a stable and structured routine, fostering emotional and developmental security.

Raised concerns about LDW’s health, such as potential allergies and unexplained injuries, and
advocated for prompt medical attention.
Ensured LDW’s material needs are met, including clothing, shoes, and weather-appropriate items.

Proposed consistent daycare arrangements and holiday plans to provide stability for LDW.
Invited Emily to attend co-parenting classes and engage in open discussions to address conflicts
(e.g., September 10, 2024).

books, singing songs, and engaging in creative play.

for his psychological health.
Respecting Court Orders:
Consistently adhered to court-ordered parenting schedules and sought legal remedies when Emily
violated these orders.
Fulfilled all financial obligations, including child support payments, despite challenges caused by
Emily’s actions.
Key Contrasts
Consistency vs. Manipulation:
I have demonstrated consistency in fostering LDW’s emotional security, while Emily’s actions disrupt
his stability through manipulation and alienation.
Collaboration vs. Obstruction:
I have made continuous efforts to collaborate with Emily for LDW’s benefit, whereas she has refused
co-parenting initiatives and withheld critical information.
Nurturing vs. Alienating:
My parenting approach prioritizes nurturing LDW’s relationship with both parents, while Emily’s
behavior actively alienates LDW from me and exposes him to unnecessary conflict.
This stark contrast underscores my commitment to LDW’s best interests and the need for custody
modifications to protect his emotional and psychological well-being.

### **8. Ongoing Alienation and Barriers to Exercising My Rights as a Father**
29. Since my forced and, I believe, illegal eviction through a PPO orchestrated by Emily, I have
been increasingly alienated from LDW’s life. This eviction has severely limited my ability to
exercise my inherent rights as a parent, despite my unwavering dedication to being a great father.
Emily and her family have created obstacles at every step, making it difficult to maintain my role
in LDW’s life.
30. **Barriers to Involvement and Parental Rights**: I have made every effort to meet the court’s
expectations, jumping through numerous legal and personal hurdles to stay connected to LDW and to
ensure his well-being. Despite my compliance and consistency, Emily continues to interfere with my
time with LDW, seemingly aiming to eliminate me from his life, much as she did with her previous
partner, Austin Muratori. This pattern of behavior reveals a focus on control over LDW, as well as
on securing the financial benefits of sole custody.
31. **Commitment to Overcoming Obstacles**: Each day, I do everything within my power to fulfill my
role as LDW’s father. I have maintained stable housing, full-time employment, and a safe home
environment for him, yet Emily’s actions limit my ability to provide the hands-on care and emotional
support I know LDW needs. Despite my consistent efforts, I am constantly met with resistance,
further isolating me from my son.
32. **Inherent Rights as a Father**: I am a capable, loving father with an established bond with
LDW, and I have the right to be an active part of his life. Emily’s continued alienation tactics not
only harm our relationship but also deprive LDW of the stability and security that comes from a
balanced, two-parent relationship.

--- PAGE 214 ---

33. **Pattern of Alienation for Control and Financial Gain**: Emily’s actions indicate a desire for
total control and financial benefit, at the expense of LDW’s well-being and our relationship. My
consistent dedication as a father, combined with her ongoing efforts to obstruct our bond,
highlights the urgent need for a fair custody modification that ensures LDW has access to both
parents.
### **9. Conclusion and Request for Relief**
34. Based on my stable home, consistent employment, unwavering commitment to LDW, and the alienation
I have faced, I respectfully request that this Court reinstate the 50/50 custody arrangement
initially recommended by the Friend of the Court. I also request an adjustment to parenting time and
child support, to accurately reflect both parents’ responsibilities and financial situations. This
modification will support LDW’s need for a balanced, secure relationship with both parents, free
from manipulation and undue control.
I affirm that the above statements are true to the best of my knowledge and belief.

# MICHIGAN SUPREME COURT - ORIGINAL ACTION

**Court:** Michigan Supreme Court
**Lower Court:** 14th Circuit Court, Muskegon County, Michigan
**Case Numbers:** 2023-5907-PP (PPO); 2024-001507-DC (Custody/Parenting Time/Child Support)
**Judge:** Hon. Jenny L. McNeill
**Petitioner:** Andrew Pigors, 1977 Whitehall Rd, Laketon Township, MI 49445
**Respondent:** Emily Watson, 2160 Garland Dr, Norton Shores, MI 49441

---

## I. JURISDICTION AND VEHICLE

This Court has original jurisdiction under Const 1963, art 6, § 4 and MCR 7.303 to grant extraordinary writs including superintending control, mandamus, and prohibition. This action is brought as an original action because:

1. The systemic violations documented below constitute judicial misconduct requiring Supreme Court intervention;
2. The pattern of due process violations threatens immediate and irreparable harm to Petitioner's parental rights;
3. Court of Appeals review would be inadequate given the urgency and scope of violations.

## III. ISSUES PRESENTED FOR ORIGINAL JURISDICTION

1. **Pattern of Judicial Misconduct**: Whether the trial court's systematic violations of procedural rules and constitutional rights warrant Supreme Court intervention under MCR 7.303.

2. **Parental Rights Emergency**: Whether immediate Supreme Court action is required to protect Petitioner's fundamental parental rights from ongoing violations.

3. **Judicial Ethics Violations**: Whether the trial court's conduct violates the Michigan Code of Judicial Conduct requiring disqualification and referral to the Judicial Tenure Commission.

4. **Systemic Due Process Failure**: Whether the trial court's pattern of ex parte orders, denial of hearings, and evidentiary gatekeeping constitutes systemic due process violation requiring extraordinary relief.

---

## IV. RELIEF REQUESTED

Petitioner respectfully requests that this Court exercise its original jurisdiction to:

1. **Issue writ of superintending control** directing the trial court to vacate all improper orders;

2. **Order immediate disqualification** of Judge McNeill and assignment of new judge;

3. **Restore Petitioner's parental rights** pending fair hearing;

4. **Refer Judge McNeill** to the Judicial Tenure Commission for investigation;

5. **Establish supervisory protocols** for the 14th Circuit Family Division;

6. **Award costs and fees**;

7. **Grant such other relief** as justice requires.

---
